The sequencer sweeps nacelle servos at 45\u00b0/s while simultaneously ramping forward fan thrust from 0% to 60%. Wing fan thrust is maintained at hover level during transition to preserve altitude. Options:\n   - For analog FPV: just passthrough the video signal, no processing needed on Pico\n   - For digital FPV (DJI O3/Caddx): these use a UART for control/config\n   - For a camera that outputs video to a separate VTX: analog passthrough + UART control\n   - Could use an OV2640 or similar via SPI/I2C but that's very low res\n   - Most practical: JST-GH connector for analog camera video out + UART control lines\n\n2. **CAN FD** - Need a CAN FD controller IC (MCP2518FD via SPI) + CAN transceiver (MCP2562FD or TCAN1042)\n\n3. **Ethernet** - Need an SPI Ethernet controller (W5500 or ENC28J60). W5500 supports up to 80MHz SPI and has hardware TCP/IP stack.\n\n4. **TPM** - TPM 2.0 chip like ATTPM20P or Infineon SLB9670. Usually SPI interface. For a drone this is unusual but could be for secure boot/key storage.\n\n5. **GPS** - u-blox M10 via UART\n\n6. **IMU** - ICM-42688-P via SPI\n\n7. **Barometer** - BMP388 via I2C\n\n**SPI bus sharing strategy:**\nThe Pico 2 has 2 SPI controllers. We can share:\n- SPI0: IMU (ICM-42688-P), CAN FD controller (MCP2518FD), TPM (via CS selection)\n- SPI1: Ethernet (W5500), potentially others\n\nActually let me reconsider. The W5500 needs dedicated fast SPI. Let me plan:\n- SPI0 (up to 62.5MHz): IMU (CS0), CAN FD MCP2518FD (CS1), TPM (CS2)\n- SPI1 (up to 62.5MHz): W5500 Ethernet (CS0)\n- I2C0: BMP388 barometer\n- I2C1: spare / EEPROM for board ID\n- UART0: GPS (u-blox M10)\n- UART1: MAVLink radio (as before)\n- PWM: ESCs, servos (as before)\n\n**FPV Camera:**\nFor a drone hat, the most practical FPV camera interface is:\n- Analog: coax/JST-GH for power + video signal, straight passthrough to VTX\n- Or UART control for digital cameras\n- We could include a JST-GH connector with: GND, +5V, Video_in, Video_out, UART_TX, UART_RX\n\n**JST-GH connectors** - standard in drone/autopilot world (Pixhawk standard). Standard pinouts:\n- GPS: 6-pin JST-GH (GND, +5V, TX, RX, SDA, SCL)\n- UART: 4-pin or 6-pin\n- CAN: 4-pin JST-GH (GND, +5V, CANH, CANL)\n- I2C: 4-pin JST-GH\n- Power: 6-pin JST-GH\n\n**TPM** - Infineon SLB9670 or similar SPI TPM 2.0. For a micro drone this is unusual but it's a security feature for authenticated firmware/key storage.\n\n**Board size** - Pico 2 is 51mm \u00d7 21mm. They may include context about the purpose, audience, or technical constraints.\n    10\t\n    11\t## Design Thinking\n    12\t\n    13\tBefore coding, understand the context and commit to a BOLD aesthetic direction:\n    14\t- **Purpose**: What problem does this interface solve? Who uses it?\n    15\t- **Tone**: Pick an extreme: brutally minimal, maximalist chaos, retro-futuristic, organic/natural, luxury/refined, playful/toy-like, editorial/magazine, brutalist/raw, art deco/geometric, soft/pastel, industrial/utilitarian, etc. There are so many flavors to choose from. Use these for inspiration but design one that is true to the aesthetic direction.\n    16\t- **Constraints**: Technical requirements (framework, performance, accessibility).\n    17\t- **Differentiation**: What makes this UNFORGETTABLE? Each gets a dedicated software chip-select (GP14, GP15, GP17). ICM-42688-P uses the hardware CSn (GP17) for fastest transactions; the others use software-toggled GPIOs. Power (+5V) is switched via a small P-channel FET controlled by GP24 so the camera can be power-cycled in firmware. For OSD or digital camera control (DJI O3, Caddx Vista, HDZero), use the PIO-UART lines (GP24/25).\" },\n    { heading:\"CAN FD Bus\", color:C.orange, body:\"MCP2518FD supports both Classical CAN (1Mbps) and CAN FD (up to 8Mbps data phase). A 120\u03a9 termination resistor is footprinted with a solder bridge JP1 \u2014 populate only if this node is a bus endpoint. Supports DroneCAN / UAVCANv1 for ESC, GPS, and airspeed sensor integration.\" },\n    { heading:\"Ethernet Use Case\", color:C.purple, body:\"W5500 provides hardware TCP/IP offload with 8 independent sockets. On a drone, Ethernet is primarily useful for: (1) pre-flight log upload / config over a tethered connection, (2) direct UDP streaming to a ground station laptop on the same subnet, (3) integration with companion computers (RPi, Jetson) over a short cable. Not intended for airborne wireless \u2014 pair with a WiFi-to-Ethernet bridge module if needed. The W5500 runs up to 80MHz SPI, leaving most of SPI1 bandwidth headroom.\" },\n    { heading:\"TPM 2.0 Integration\", color:C.yellow, body:\"The SLB9670 provides hardware-backed key storage and attestation. With RP2350's TrustZone-M, the Pico 2 can boot into a secure world, derive keys from the TPM, and attest firmware integrity before running the flight control loop. Practical uses: encrypted MAVLink streams, signed firmware updates, flight log tamper detection. Requires TPM 2.0 software stack \u2014 port tpm2-tss lightweight library or use Infineon's embedded TPM API.\" },\n    { heading:\"Power Architecture\", color:C.yellow, body:\"VSYS rail (+5V from BEC via J8) feeds: Pico 2 VSYS pin, MCP2562FD VBUS, and AP2112K-3.3 input. The AP2112K derives a clean 3.3V for all sensors (IMU, baro, GPS, W5500, TPM, CAN controller). A 100\u03bcF bulk cap on VSYS and 10\u03bcF + 100nF per IC. VBAT (raw LiPo) is monitored via GP26/ADC0 through a 100k/10k divider (\u00d70.091 ratio, 16.8V max \u2192 1.53V at ADC). Never connect raw LiPo to any IC supply pin.\" },\n    { heading:\"PCB Stackup\", color:C.dim, body:\"4-layer: TOP (signals + components), GND plane (layer 2), PWR plane (layer 3), BOTTOM (signals). Keep IMU routing on TOP with ground guard ring. Route SPI0 and SPI1 on separate layers where they cross. Place 100nF decoupling caps within 0.5mm of each IC supply pin on TOP layer. GPS module requires a keepout from digital clock traces to maintain RF sensitivity \u2014 place on top-center with U.FL at board edge.\" },\n  ];\n  return (\n    <div>\n      {notes.map((n,i) => (\n Power (+5V) is switched via a small P-channel FET controlled by GP24 so the camera can be power-cycled in firmware. For OSD or digital camera control (DJI O3, Caddx Vista, HDZero), use the PIO-UART lines (GP24/25).\" },\n    { heading:\"CAN FD Bus\", color:C.orange, body:\"MCP2518FD supports both Classical CAN (1Mbps) and CAN FD (up to 8Mbps data phase). The MCP2562FD transceiver is a 3.3V-logic / 5V-bus split-supply device. CANH and CANL are protected by SMAJ5.0A TVS diodes. A 120\u03a9 termination resistor is footprinted with a solder bridge JP1 \u2014 populate only if this node is a bus endpoint. Supports DroneCAN / UAVCANv1 for ESC, GPS, and airspeed sensor integration.\" },\n    { heading:\"Ethernet Use Case\", color:C.purple, body:\"W5500 provides hardware TCP/IP offload with 8 independent sockets. On a drone, Ethernet is primarily useful for: (1) pre-flight log upload / config over a tethered connection, (2) direct UDP streaming to a ground station laptop on the same subnet, (3) integration with companion computers (RPi, Jetson) over a short cable. Not intended for airborne wireless \u2014 pair with a WiFi-to-Ethernet bridge module if needed. The W5500 runs up to 80MHz SPI, leaving most of SPI1 bandwidth headroom.\" },\n    { heading:\"TPM 2.0 Integration\", color:C.yellow, body:\"The SLB9670 provides hardware-backed key storage and attestation. With RP2350's TrustZone-M, the Pico 2 can boot into a secure world, derive keys from the TPM, and attest firmware integrity before running the flight control loop. Practical uses: encrypted MAVLink streams, signed firmware updates, flight log tamper detection. Requires TPM 2.0 software stack \u2014 port tpm2-tss lightweight library or use Infineon's embedded TPM API.\" },\n    { heading:\"Power Architecture\", color:C.yellow, body:\"VSYS rail (+5V from BEC via J8) feeds: Pico 2 VSYS pin, MCP2562FD VBUS, and AP2112K-3.3 input. The AP2112K derives a clean 3.3V for all sensors (IMU, baro, GPS, W5500, TPM, CAN controller). A 100\u03bcF bulk cap on VSYS and 10\u03bcF + 100nF per IC. VBAT (raw LiPo) is monitored via GP26/ADC0 through a 100k/10k divider (\u00d70.091 ratio, 16.8V max \u2192 1.53V at ADC). Never connect raw LiPo to any IC supply pin.\" },\n    { heading:\"PCB Stackup\", color:C.dim, body:\"4-layer: TOP (signals + components), GND plane (layer 2), PWR plane (layer 3), BOTTOM (signals). Keep IMU routing on TOP with ground guard ring. Route SPI0 and SPI1 on separate layers where they cross. Place 100nF decoupling caps within 0.5mm of each IC supply pin on TOP layer. Here's how the key design decisions were made:\n\n**All sensors on-board:** The u-blox M10Q GPS is a complete module (~9.6\u00d79.6mm) with a built-in patch antenna and U.FL footprint for an external antenna. A solder jumper selects whether UART0 routes to the on-board M10Q or the external J5 JST-GH port \u2014 so you can swap to a higher-spec GPS later without a redesign.\n\n**SPI0 bus sharing:** The ICM-42688-P IMU, MCP2518FD CAN FD controller, and SLB9670 TPM all share SPI0 (GP16\u201319) with independent chip-selects. The IMU gets the hardware CSn (GP17) for lowest latency; CAN and TPM use software-toggled GPIOs. Keep SPI0 stubs under 15mm to avoid reflections at 24MHz.\n\n**FPV camera:** The Pico 2 has no ADC fast enough for video \u2014 so the hat is a passive video passthrough (camera \u2192 VID_IN \u2192 VID_OUT \u2192 VTX), no processing at all. A P-FET on the camera +5V line lets firmware power-cycle it. PIO state machines on GP24/25 implement a software UART for OSD or digital camera control (DJI, HDZero, Caddx).\n\n**CAN FD** at up to 8Mbps with a footprinted 120\u03a9 termination solder bridge \u2014 populate only if this node is a bus endpoint. Supports DroneCAN/UAVCANv1 for future ESC or airspeed sensor integration.\n\n**Ethernet** via W5500 is primarily for ground-side config uploads, log streaming, or companion computer (RPi/Jetson) integration \u2014 not airborne comms.\n\n**TPM** ties into RP2350's TrustZone-M for firmware attestation, encrypted MAVLink, and signed OTA updates. To use GPIO14/15 for SiK radio (which needs reliable UART), we should disable Bluetooth or swap UART assignments in config.txt.\n\nBetter plan:\n- Disable Bluetooth (dtoverlay=disable-bt) \u2192 GPIO14/15 become UART0 (PL011, reliable)\n- Use GPIO14/15 for SiK MAVLink radio\n- Use SPI0 for CAN FD + W5500 + TPM (with software CS via extra GPIOs)\n- Use SPI1 for 49MHz transceiver SPI interface + extra SD card\n- I2C0: Hat EEPROM\n- I2C1: spare / sensors\n\nThis is feasible.\n\nFor the 4GB RAM issue: I'll note it and suggest either accepting 512MB (sufficient for MAVLink routing, video processing, and mission planning) or upgrading to CM4 Lite + custom carrier board.\n\nNow let me think about the **weight and balance recalculation**.\n\n**Component weights:**\n\nOriginal system:\n- Airframe (CF tubes, printed shell, landing gear): ~80g\n- 2\u00d7 40mm ducted fans + motors: 2 \u00d7 ~30g = ~60g\n- 2\u00d7 nacelle servos (MG90S): 2 \u00d7 9g = ~18g\n- 2\u00d7 ESC 20A: 2 \u00d7 ~10g = ~20g\n- 1\u00d7 30mm forward fan + motor: ~15g\n- 1\u00d7 ESC 20A (fwd): ~8g\n- Pico 2 + sensor hat: ~15g (Pico ~3g + hat PCB + components ~12g)\n- SiK radio: ~20g\n- 4S 1300mAh LiPo: ~100g\n- Wiring/connectors: ~20g\n- **Original total: ~356g \u2248 say 360g** (they said ~420g originally, let me use that)\n\nActually I said AUW ~420g originally. For a tiltrotor in cruise, the CG should ideally be at or slightly ahead of the aerodynamic center. For hover, CG at wing line is ideal for neutral stability.\n\nCG at 138mm is 22mm ahead of wing pivot (160mm). This means the aircraft is slightly nose-heavy, which is generally desirable for stability in cruise. However, for hover in a tiltrotor, this means the nose will tend to pitch down, requiring slight forward tilt of nacelles or more thrust from the fuselage fan to compensate.\n\nBattery position can be adjusted to trim CG. Here's the summary of key design decisions and trade-offs:\n\n**Why CM4 Lite (no eMMC)?** The Lite variant lets the carrier provide a standard microSD slot for the OS \u2014 easier to reflash in the field, no special tools. The COMPHAT-1's separate log SD remains completely independent on SPI1.\n\n**The \"Zero-sized\" constraint:** Unavoidable compromise \u2014 the CM4 module is 55\u00d740mm, so the carrier has to be **65\u00d740mm** (same 65mm length as a Zero, but 10mm wider). That's the physical minimum to fit the two Hirose DF40C-100 connectors. The COMPHAT-1 is already 65\u00d748mm, so the fuselage bay envelope doesn't change. Mounting hole spacing matches Pi Zero (58mm \u00d7 23mm diagonal) so the stack drops into the same standoff pattern.\n\n**CM4 sandwich orientation:** The CM4 module plugs into the underside of the carrier via the DF40 connectors. The carrier's top face is clean \u2014 just the 40-pin GPIO header for COMPHAT-1, the OS microSD slot, and the WiFi antenna keepout zone. Stack height is ~22mm total.\n\n**Recalculated numbers:**\n- **AUW: 644g** (+14g vs the Pi Zero 2W design)\n- **T/W: 2.02:1** \u2014 still comfortably above the 1.8:1 VTOL minimum\n- **Hover throttle: ~50%** \u2014 excellent margin\n- **Hover endurance: ~6.1 min** (5S 2200mAh, 80% usable) \u2014 slide to 5S 3000mAh for ~8.3 min\n- **CG shift: +5mm aft** \u2014 corrected by sliding the battery rail ~18mm aft; add a 10g nose slug if rail travel runs out\n\n**COMPHAT-1 needs zero changes** \u2014 the CM4's 40-pin GPIO header is electrically identical to the Pi Zero's.",

MatrixTab() {\n  // rows = tx, cols = other; values = separation + notes\n  const ants = [\n    {k:\"gps\",  label:\"GPS L1\"},\n    {k:\"sik\",  label:\"SiK 915\"},\n    {k:\"rc49\", label:\"49      );\n                })}\n              </tr>\n            ))}\n          </tbody>\n        </table>\n      </div>\n      <Note c={C.green} ch=\"All separation requirements met. Place ferrite beads (Fair-Rite 0443164151) on each ESC power lead. Add a 100nF + 10\u03bcF decoupling cap at each ESC input. The GPS patch is 58mm from the nose \u2014 the nearest EDF is at the wing tip (>300mm away). The SiK whip at 238mm is 60mm from the CF spar but 300mm+ from any motor.     "text": "Click any antenna in the three-view diagram to inspect it. Key decisions explained:\n\n**GPS patch \u2014 58mm from nose, top surface**\nThe most forward position keeps it 232mm from the 49 MHz loading coil (the biggest threat to GPS LNA noise floor) and well above the payload bay and skid gear. Raised 12mm on a PLA standoff to clear the access hatch hinges. The pitot tube sits ~50mm below the patch plane \u2014 negligible interference at L1.\n\n**SiK 915 MHz \u2014 238mm from nose, belly**\nBelly-mounted so the toroidal beam pattern points naturally toward the ground station. Positioned 43mm aft of the payload bay rear edge \u2014 the payload door and winch hook are clear. Being on the *opposite face* from the 49 MHz antenna gives about 18 dB of additional isolation on top of their 52mm axial separation, which is what makes that pairing workable.\n\n**49 MHz RCRS \u2014 290mm from nose, dorsal fin, top surface**\nThe hardest antenna on the aircraft. \u03bb/4 at 49 MHz is **1530 mm** \u2014 physically impossible at this scale. The solution is a **250mm whip + 38 \u03bcH base-loading coil on a #43 ferrite rod**, which electrically resonates the short element to \u03bb/4. Efficiency drops to roughly \u22126 to \u22129 dB versus a full-size antenna, but at \u226410 mW EIRP and \u2264500m TDDS range that's fine \u2014 link margin analysis in the 49 MHz TDDS spec still closes comfortably. Four 150 mm counterpoise radials substitute for a ground plane on the plastic fuselage. The dorsal fin keeps it entirely clear of the winch mechanism.\n\n**WiFi \u2014 internal, 210mm, no installation steps**\nThe CM4 PCB trace antenna radiates through the PLA shell with 2\u20133 dB insertion loss. Only used for bench SSH and QGC backup \u2014 no range requirement beyond 80m.\n\n**Critical bench test before flight:** spin the EDFs at hover throttle and verify GPS HDOP stays \u22641.5, and connect a nanoVNA to the 49 MHz antenna to confirm SWR \u22642.5:1 across all six RCRS channels with the airframe closed up.",

Contains: pitot port, GPS patch on top, access hatch for Pico 2/TRIHAT-1\n- **Main oval hull**: Primary avionics/battery bay. CM4 stack, COMPHAT-1, battery on rail\n- **Side lateral outriggers** (the two struts): Become the wing spars/nacelle arms. Grid(){return(\n  <svg style={{position:\"fixed\",inset:0,width:\"100%\",height:\"100%\",pointerEvents:\"none\",zIndex:0}}>\n    <defs>\n      <pattern id=\"sg\" width=\"20\" height=\"20\" patternUnits=\"userSpaceOnUse\">\n        <path d=\"M20 0L0 0 0 20\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.035)\" strokeWidth={0.5}/>\n      </pattern>\n      <pattern id=\"lg\" width=\"100\" height=\"100\" patternUnits=\"userSpaceOnUse\">\n        <rect width=\"100\" height=\"100\" fill=\"url(#sg)\"/>\n        <path d=\"M100 0L0 0 0 100\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.065)\" strokeWidth={1}/>\n      </pattern>\n    </defs>\n    <rect width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\" fill=\"url(#lg)\"/>\n  </svg>\n);}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n//  SERENITY HULL GEOMETRY \u2014 all in px, nose at left\n//  Scale: 1 px \u2248 0.72 mm  \u2192  320mm hull = 444px\n//  Total length including engine pod: 360mm = 500px\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// X positions (from nose, in px)\nconst S = (mm) => mm * 1.30;      // scale: 1.30 px/mm\nconst NX  = 55;                    // nose tip x\nconst x   = (mm) => NX + S(mm);   // nose-relative x\n\n// KEY X stations (mm from nose):\nconst X_COCKPIT_END   = x(88);    // end of cockpit bubble\nconst X_STRUT_FWD     = x(110);   // outrigger arm forward junction\nconst X_STRUT_AFT     = x(175);   // outrigger arm aft junction\nconst X_HULL_MAX      = x(140);   // maximum hull beam\nconst X_BATTERY_CTR   = x(185);   // battery centroid\nconst X_PAYLOAD_FWD   = x(130);   // payload bay forward\nconst X_PAYLOAD_AFT   = x(200);   // payload bay aft\nconst X_NECK_START    = x(220);   // hull narrows to engine neck\nconst X_NECK_END      = x(260);   // neck end / engine bell start\nconst X_ENGINE_CTR    = x(300);   // 30mm EDF centre\nconst X_TAIL          = x(360);   // extreme tail\n\n// CG & pivot\nconst X_CG     = x(152);   // target CG\nconst X_PIVOT  = x(160);   // wing pivot / neutral point\n\n// \u2500\u2500 SERENITY TOP-VIEW PATH \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Hull outline \u2014 smooth Bezier approximation of the Serenity silhouette\nfunction TopHullPath(){\n  const CY = 0; // relative to hull centreline\n  // nose tip \u2192 cockpit bulge \u2192 waist \u2192 max beam \u2192 taper \u2192 neck \u2192 engine bell \u2192 tail\n  // symmetric, generate upper then reflect for lower\n  const pts = [\n    [x(0),   0],     // nose tip\n    [x(20),  18],    // nose widening\n    [x(55),  42],    // cockpit shoulder\n    [x(88),  48],    // cockpit max (side window)\n    [x(120), 55],    // main hull max beam region\n    [x(160), 52],    // battery bay\n    [x(220), 38],    // hull taper starts\n    [x(255), 24],    // neck\n    [x(280), 32],    // engine bell widens\n    [x(320), 38],    // engine bell max\n    [x(360), 28],    // engine exit / tail\n  ];\n  // Build SVG smooth path (upper half, mirrored for lower)\n  let d = `M ${NX} 0 `;\n  // upper hull\n  for(let i=1;i<pts.length;i++){\n    const [px,py]=pts[i];\n    const [qx,qy]=pts[i-1];\n    const cx=(qx+px)/2; const cy=(qy+py)/2;\n    d += `Q ${qx} ${qy} ${cx} ${cy} `;\n  }\n  d += `Q ${pts[pts.length-2][0]} ${pts[pts.length-2][1]} ${pts[pts.length-1][0]} ${pts[pts.length-1][1]} `;\n  return {upper:pts, path:d};\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 TOP VIEW SVG \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction TopView({sel,onSel}){\n  const VW=740, VH=340, CY=170;\n  const H=(mm)=>CY-S(mm); // y for +beam\n  const L=(mm)=>CY+S(mm); // y for -beam\n\n  // Hull half-widths at key stations (mm from nose)\n  const profile=[\n    [0,0],[8,10],[22,18],[40,30],[58,36],[88,37],\n    [120,42],[140,42],[165,40],[190,36],[220,29],\n    [252,18],[260,16],[278,24],[305,29],[330,28],[360,22],\n  ];\n  const upper = profile.map(([xmm,ymm])=>[x(xmm), CY-S(ymm)]);\n  const lower = [...profile].reverse().map(([xmm,ymm])=>[x(xmm), CY+S(ymm)]);\n  const allPts=[...upper,...lower];\n  const outline=allPts.map((p,i)=>i===0?`M${p[0]},${p[1]}`:`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \")+\"Z\";\n\n  // Outrigger arms (the Serenity's lateral struts)\n  // Junction at x(130)\u2013x(175), extends to 340mm from centreline each side\n  const ARM_Y_SIDE  = S(340); // 340mm from centreline\n  const ARM_Y_INNER = S(46);  // where arm meets hull\n\n  // Nacelle pods at arm tips: 60mm EDF duct, oval top view\n  const N_RX=S(32), N_RY=S(14); // nacelle oval half-widths\n\n  // Cockpit dome footprint\n  const ckpX=x(44), ckpY=S(26);\n\n  // Highlighted zones\n  const zones=[\n    {id:\"cockpit\",  lbl:\"COCKPIT / SENSOR BAY\",   x1:x(0),  x2:x(88),  c:C.teal},\n    {id:\"avionics\", lbl:\"AVIONICS\",               x1:x(60), x2:x(160), c:C.accent},\n    {id:\"battery\",  lbl:\"BATTERY RAIL\",            x1:x(140),x2:x(230), c:C.yellow},\n    {id:\"payload\",  lbl:\"PAYLOAD BAY (BELLY)\",     x1:x(130),x2:x(200), c:C.pink},\n    {id:\"engine\",   lbl:\"FWD EDF (30mm)\",          x1:x(270),x2:x(330), c:C.orange},\n  ];\n\n  return(\n    <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${VW} ${VH}`} width=\"100%\" style={{maxWidth:\"100%\",display:\"block\"}}>\n      <defs>\n        <clipPath id=\"tvclip\"><rect x={0} y={0} width={VW} height={VH}/></clipPath>\n      </defs>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Zone overlays \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {zones.map(z=>(\n        <rect key={z.id} x={z.x1} y={CY-S(46)} width={z.x2-z.x1} height={S(92)}\n          fill={`${z.c}12`} stroke={z.c} strokeWidth={0.7} strokeDasharray=\"5 3\" opacity={0.7}\n          rx={3} style={{cursor:\"pointer\"}} onClick={()=>onSel(sel===z.id?null:z.id)}/>\n      ))}\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Hull outline \u2500\u2500 */}\n      <path d={outline} fill={C.hull} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.8}/>\n\n      {/* Cockpit dome footprint */}\n      <ellipse cx={ckpX} cy={CY} rx={S(44)} ry={ckpY}\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.08)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1}/>\n\n      {/* Dorsal ridge line */}\n      <line x1={x(30)} y1={CY} x2={x(280)} y2={CY}\n        stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.25)\" strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"8 4\"/>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Outrigger arms \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {[-1,1].map(side=>{\n        const sy=CY+side*ARM_Y_SIDE;\n        const iy=CY+side*ARM_Y_INNER;\n        // arm tapers from hull to tip\n        const aPts=[\n          [x(115), CY+side*S(42)],\n          [x(128), CY+side*S(48)],\n          [x(152), CY+side*S(180)],\n          [x(160), sy],\n          [x(175), sy],\n          [x(185), CY+side*S(175)],\n          [x(196), CY+side*S(48)],\n        ];\n        const fwd=`M${aPts[0][0]},${aPts[0][1]} `;\n        const afwd=aPts.slice(1,4).map(p=>`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \");\n        const abck=aPts.slice(4).reverse().map(p=>`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \");\n        const armPath=fwd+afwd+\" \"+abck+\"Z\";\n        return(\n          <g key={side}>\n            <path d={armPath} fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.05)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.3}/>\n            {/* CF spar tube line */}\n            <line x1={x(130)} y1={CY+side*S(50)} x2={x(170)} y2={sy-side*S(4)}\n              stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.35)\" strokeWidth={2} strokeDasharray=\"6 3\"/>\n            {/* Nacelle EDF pod */}\n            <ellipse cx={x(155)} cy={sy} rx={N_RX} ry={N_RY}\n              fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.12)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={1.5}/>\n            {/* Fan inlet circle */}\n            <circle cx={x(155)} cy={sy} r={S(20)}\n              fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.08)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\"/>\n            {/* Tilt axis indicator */}\n            <line x1={x(130)} y1={sy} x2={x(180)} y2={sy}\n              stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\" opacity={0.6}/>\n            <text x={x(155)} y={sy+(side>0?14:-18)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n              fill={C.orange} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>{side<0?\"NACELLE L\":\"NACELLE R\"}</text>\n          </g>\n        );\n      })}\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Engine bell \u2500\u2500 */}\n      <ellipse cx={X_ENGINE_CTR} cy={CY} rx={S(18)} ry={S(18)}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,230,0,0.1)\" stroke={C.yellow} strokeWidth={1.5}/>\n      <circle cx={X_ENGINE_CTR} cy={CY} r={S(10)}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,230,0,0.15)\" stroke={C.yellow} strokeWidth={1}/>\n      <text x={X_ENGINE_CTR} y={CY+3} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.yellow} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>EDF</text>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Pitot {/* \u2500\u2500 Antenna markers \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {/* GPS patch */}\n      <rect x={x(46)} y={CY-S(14)} width={S(24)} height={S(10)}\n        fill=\"rgba(74,222,128,0.2)\" stroke=\"#4ade80\" strokeWidth={1}/>\n      <text x={x(58)} y={CY-S(18)} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill=\"#4ade80\" fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>GPS</text>\n      {/* 49MHz dorsal */}\n      <circle cx={x(290)} cy={CY-S(16)} r={4}\n        fill=\"rgba(244,114,182,0.2)\" stroke={C.pink} strokeWidth={1}/>\n      <text x={x(290)} y={CY-S(22)} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.pink} fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>49M\u2191</text>\n      {/* SiK belly */}\n      <circle cx={x(238)} cy={CY} r={4}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.15)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"2 2\"/>\n      <text x={x(238)} y={CY+12} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.orange} fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>SiK\u2193</text>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 CG & pivot \u2500\u2500 */}\n      <line x1={X_CG} y1={CY-S(56)} x2={X_CG} y2={CY+S(56)}\n        stroke={C.green} strokeWidth={1} strokeDasharray=\"5 3\"/>\n      <polygon points={`${X_CG},${CY-S(56)} ${X_CG-7},${CY-S(36)} ${X_CG+7},${CY-S(36)}`}\n        fill={C.green} opacity={0.9}/>\n      <text x={X_CG} y={CY-S(62)} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.green} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>CG\u00b7152</text>\n\n      {/* Zone labels */}\n      {sel && zones.filter(z=>z.id===sel).map(z=>(\n        <text key={z.id} x={(z.x1+z.x2)/2} y={CY-S(52)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n          fill={z.c} fontSize={9} fontFamily={M} fontWeight=\"bold\">{z.lbl}</text>\n      ))}\n\n      {/* Dim line */}\n      <line x1={NX} y1={VH-18} x2={X_TAIL} y2={VH-18} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <line x1={NX} y1={VH-22} x2={NX} y2={VH-14} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <line x1={X_TAIL} y1={VH-22} x2={X_TAIL} y2={VH-14} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <text x={(NX+X_TAIL)/2} y={VH-7} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>360 mm</text>\n\n      {/* Wingspan dim */}\n      <line x1={NX+S(25)} y1={CY-S(350)} x2={NX+S(25)} y2={CY+S(350)}\n        stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.15}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(25)-8} y={CY} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}\n        transform={`rotate(-90 ${NX+S(25)-8} ${CY})`}>680mm wingspan</text>\n\n      <text x={VW/2} y={16} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.25)\"\n        fontSize={9} fontFamily={M} letterSpacing=\"0.12em\">TOP / PLAN VIEW \u2014 CLICK ZONE TO IDENTIFY</text>\n      <text x={NX-8} y={CY+4} textAnchor=\"end\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>NOSE</text>\n      <text x={X_TAIL+5} y={CY+4} fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>TAIL</text>\n    </svg>\n  );\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 SIDE VIEW SVG \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction SideView(){\n  const VW=680, VH=320, BY=180; // BY = bottom of fuselage baseline\n\n  // Side profile half-heights (above and below centre) at key x stations (mm)\n  // Serenity side: forward cockpit bubble tall, hull sweeps, neck thin, engine bell re-expands\n  const above=[ // top edge\n    [0,0],[5,8],[18,22],[40,32],[58,38],[75,36],\n    [88,30],[110,26],[140,26],[165,25],[195,24],\n    [220,20],[255,12],[270,16],[300,20],[340,18],[360,14],\n  ];\n  const below=[ // bottom edge (belly)\n    [0,0],[10,-5],[35,-14],[88,-20],[140,-22],[180,-22],\n    [220,-20],[255,-14],[270,-18],[300,-22],[340,-20],[360,-14],\n  ];\n  const buildPath=(pts,flip=false)=>{\n    return pts.map(([xmm,ymm],i)=>{\n      const px=NX+S(xmm), py=BY-S(ymm)*(flip?-1:1);\n      return i===0?`M${px},${py}`:`L${px},${py}`;\n    }).join(\" \");\n  };\n  const topEdge=buildPath(above);\n  const botEdge=buildPath(below.map(([x,y])=>[x,-y])); // flip for below\n  const outlineTop=above.map(([xmm,ymm])=>[NX+S(xmm), BY-S(ymm)]);\n  const outlineBot=[...below].reverse().map(([xmm,ymm])=>[NX+S(xmm), BY+S(Math.abs(ymm))]);\n  const allSide=[...outlineTop,...outlineBot];\n  const sidePath=allSide.map((p,i)=>i===0?`M${p[0]},${p[1]}`:`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \")+\"Z\";\n\n  return(\n    <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${VW} ${VH}`} width=\"100%\" style={{maxWidth:\"100%\",display:\"block\"}}>\n      {/* Hull */}\n      <path d={sidePath} fill={C.hull} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.8}/>\n\n      {/* Cockpit bubble \u2014 the iconic raised dome of the Serenity */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(8)},${BY-S(22)} Q${NX+S(45)},${BY-S(65)} ${NX+S(85)},${BY-S(30)}`}\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.1)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.2}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(44)} y={BY-S(48)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.45)\" fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>COCKPIT</text>\n\n      {/* Outrigger junction visible as bracket on side */}\n      <line x1={NX+S(130)} y1={BY-S(26)} x2={NX+S(130)} y2={BY-S(60)}\n        stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=\"round\"/>\n      <line x1={NX+S(170)} y1={BY-S(26)} x2={NX+S(170)} y2={BY-S(60)}\n        stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=\"round\"/>\n      {/* Nacelle side profile \u2014 shown in hover (vertical) position */}\n      <rect x={NX+S(138)} y={BY-S(95)} width={S(24)} height={S(48)} rx={4}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.1)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={1.3}/>\n      {/* Fan inlet at bottom of nacelle in hover */}\n      <ellipse cx={NX+S(150)} cy={BY-S(52)} rx={S(10)} ry={S(4)}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.15)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8}/>\n      {/* Tilt arc */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(130)},${BY-S(62)} A${S(24)},${S(24)} 0 0,1 ${NX+S(154)},${BY-S(38)}`}\n        fill=\"none\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\" opacity={0.7}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(150)} y={BY-S(102)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.orange} fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>\u00b190\u00b0</text>\n      <text x={NX+S(150)} y={BY-S(110)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.orange} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M} fontWeight=\"bold\">NACELLE</text>\n\n      {/* Engine bell \u2014 iconic Serenity exhaust ring */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(265)},${BY-S(13)} Q${NX+S(275)},${BY-S(24)} ${NX+S(285)},${BY-S(22)}\n                L${NX+S(330)},${BY-S(22)} Q${NX+S(345)},${BY-S(20)} ${NX+S(355)},${BY-S(15)}\n                L${NX+S(360)},${BY-S(14)} L${NX+S(360)},${BY+S(14)}\n                L${NX+S(355)},${BY+S(15)} Q${NX+S(345)},${BY+S(20)} ${NX+S(330)},${BY+S(22)}\n                L${NX+S(285)},${BY+S(22)} Q${NX+S(275)},${BY+S(24)} ${NX+S(265)},${BY+S(13)}`}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,230,0,0.08)\" stroke={C.yellow} strokeWidth={1.3}/>\n      <circle cx={NX+S(300)} cy={BY} r={S(13)}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,230,0,0.12)\" stroke={C.yellow} strokeWidth={1}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(300)} y={BY+4} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.yellow} fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>30mm EDF</text>\n\n      {/* Payload bay belly */}\n      <rect x={NX+S(130)} y={BY+S(20)} width={S(70)} height={S(22)} rx={3}\n        fill=\"rgba(244,114,182,0.1)\" stroke={C.pink} strokeWidth={1} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\"/>\n      <text x={NX+S(165)} y={BY+S(33)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.pink} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>PAYLOAD BAY</text>\n\n      {/* Landing skids \u2014 adapted from Serenity's 3-leg style */}\n      {[x(95),x(230)].map((sx,i)=>(\n        <g key={i}>\n          <line x1={sx} y1={BY+S(20)} x2={sx-S(8)} y2={BY+S(42)}\n            stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.5} opacity={0.5}/>\n          <line height=\"100\" patternUnits=\"userSpaceOnUse\">\n        <rect width=\"100\" height=\"100\" fill=\"url(#sg)\"/>\n        <path d=\"M100 0L0 0 0 100\" fill=\"none\" stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.065)\" strokeWidth={1}/>\n      </pattern>\n    </defs>\n    <rect width=\"100%\" height=\"100%\" fill=\"url(#lg)\"/>\n  </svg>\n);}\n\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n//  SERENITY HULL GEOMETRY \u2014 all in px, nose at left\n//  Scale: 1 px \u2248 0.72 mm  \u2192  320mm hull = 444px\n//  Total length including engine pod: 360mm = 500px\n// \u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\u2550\n// X positions (from nose, in px)\nconst S = (mm) => mm * 1.30;      // scale: 1.30 px/mm\nconst NX  = 55;                    // nose tip x\nconst x   = (mm) => NX + S(mm);   // nose-relative x\n\n// KEY X stations (mm from nose):\nconst X_COCKPIT_END   = x(88);    // end of cockpit bubble\nconst X_STRUT_FWD     = x(110);   // outrigger arm forward junction\nconst X_STRUT_AFT     = x(175);   // outrigger arm aft junction\nconst X_HULL_MAX      = x(140);   // maximum hull beam\nconst X_BATTERY_CTR   = x(185);   // battery centroid\nconst X_PAYLOAD_FWD   = x(130);   // payload bay forward\nconst X_PAYLOAD_AFT   = x(200);   // payload bay aft\nconst X_NECK_START    = x(220);   // hull narrows to engine neck\nconst X_NECK_END      = x(260);   // neck end / engine bell start\nconst X_ENGINE_CTR    = x(300);   // 30mm EDF centre\nconst X_TAIL          = x(360);   // extreme tail\n\n// CG & pivot\nconst X_CG     = x(152);   // target CG\nconst X_PIVOT  = x(160);   // wing pivot / neutral point\n\n// \u2500\u2500 SERENITY TOP-VIEW PATH \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n// Hull outline \u2014 smooth Bezier approximation of the Serenity silhouette\nfunction TopHullPath(){\n  const CY = 0; // relative to hull centreline\n  // nose tip \u2192 cockpit bulge \u2192 waist \u2192 max beam \u2192 taper \u2192 neck \u2192 engine bell \u2192 tail\n  // symmetric, generate upper then reflect for lower\n  const pts = [\n    [x(0),   0],     // nose tip\n    [x(20),  18],    // nose widening\n    [x(55),  42],    // cockpit shoulder\n    [x(88),  48],    // cockpit max (side window)\n    [x(120), 55],    // main hull max beam region\n    [x(160), 52],    // battery bay\n    [x(220), 38],    // hull taper starts\n    [x(255), 24],    // neck\n    [x(280), 32],    // engine bell widens\n    [x(320), 38],    // engine bell max\n    [x(360), 28],    // engine exit / tail\n  ];\n  // Build SVG smooth path (upper half, mirrored for lower)\n  let d = `M ${NX} 0 `;\n  // upper hull\n  for(let i=1;i<pts.length;i++){\n    const [px,py]=pts[i];\n    const [qx,qy]=pts[i-1];\n    const cx=(qx+px)/2; const cy=(qy+py)/2;\n    d += `Q ${qx} ${qy} ${cx} ${cy} `;\n  }\n  d += `Q ${pts[pts.length-2][0]} ${pts[pts.length-2][1]} ${pts[pts.length-1][0]} ${pts[pts.length-1][1]} `;\n  return {upper:pts, path:d};\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 TOP VIEW SVG \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction TopView({sel,onSel}){\n  const VW=740, VH=340, CY=170;\n  const H=(mm)=>CY-S(mm); // y for +beam\n  const L=(mm)=>CY+S(mm); // y for -beam\n\n  // Hull half-widths at key stations (mm from nose)\n  const profile=[\n    [0,0],[8,10],[22,18],[40,30],[58,36],[88,37],\n    [120,42],[140,42],[165,40],[190,36],[220,29],\n    [252,18],[260,16],[278,24],[305,29],[330,28],[360,22],\n  ];\n  const upper = profile.map(([xmm,ymm])=>[x(xmm), CY-S(ymm)]);\n  const lower = [...profile].reverse().map(([xmm,ymm])=>[x(xmm), CY+S(ymm)]);\n  const allPts=[...upper,...lower];\n  const outline=allPts.map((p,i)=>i===0?`M${p[0]},${p[1]}`:`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \")+\"Z\";\n\n  // Outrigger arms (the Serenity's lateral struts)\n  // Junction at x(130)\u2013x(175), extends to 340mm from centreline each side\n  const ARM_Y_SIDE  = S(340); // 340mm from centreline\n  const ARM_Y_INNER = S(46);  // where arm meets hull\n\n  // Nacelle pods at arm tips: 60mm EDF duct, oval top view\n  const N_RX=S(32), N_RY=S(14); // nacelle oval half-widths\n\n  // Cockpit dome footprint\n  const ckpX=x(44), ckpY=S(26);\n\n  // Highlighted zones\n  const zones=[\n    {id:\"cockpit\",  lbl:\"COCKPIT / SENSOR BAY\",   x1:x(0),  x2:x(88),  c:C.teal},\n    {id:\"avionics\", lbl:\"AVIONICS\",               x1:x(60), x2:x(160), c:C.accent},\n    {id:\"battery\",  lbl:\"BATTERY RAIL\",            x1:x(140),x2:x(230), c:C.yellow},\n    {id:\"payload\",  lbl:\"PAYLOAD BAY (BELLY)\",     x1:x(130),x2:x(200), c:C.pink},\n    {id:\"engine\",   lbl:\"FWD EDF (30mm)\",          x1:x(270),x2:x(330), c:C.orange},\n  ];\n\n  return(\n    <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${VW} ${VH}`} width=\"100%\" style={{maxWidth:\"100%\",display:\"block\"}}>\n      <defs>\n        <clipPath id=\"tvclip\"><rect x={0} y={0} width={VW} height={VH}/></clipPath>\n      </defs>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Zone overlays \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {zones.map(z=>(\n        <rect key={z.id} x={z.x1} onClick={()=>onSel(sel===z.id?null:z.id)}/>\n      ))}\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Hull outline \u2500\u2500 */}\n      <path d={outline} fill={C.hull} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.8}/>\n\n      {/* Cockpit dome footprint */}\n      <ellipse cx={ckpX} cy={CY} rx={S(44)} ry={ckpY}\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.08)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1}/>\n\n      {/* Dorsal ridge line */}\n      <line x1={x(30)} y1={CY} x2={x(280)} y2={CY}\n        stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.25)\" strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"8 4\"/>\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Outrigger arms \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {[-1,1].map(side=>{\n        const sy=CY+side*ARM_Y_SIDE;\n        const iy=CY+side*ARM_Y_INNER;\n        // arm tapers from hull to tip\n        const aPts=[\n          [x(115), CY+side*S(42)],\n          [x(128), CY+side*S(48)],\n          [x(152), CY+side*S(180)],\n          [x(160), sy],\n          [x(175), sy],\n          [x(185), CY+side*S(175)],\n          [x(196), CY+side*S(48)],\n        ];\n        const fwd=`M${aPts[0][0]},${aPts[0][1]} `;\n        const afwd=aPts.slice(1,4).map(p=>`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \");\n        const abck=aPts.slice(4).reverse().map(p=>`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \");\n        const armPath=fwd+afwd+\" \"+abck+\"Z\";\n        return(\n          <g key={side}>\n            <path d={armPath} fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.05)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.3}/>\n            {/* CF spar tube line */}\n            <line x1={x(130)} y1={CY+side*S(50)} x2={x(170)} y2={sy-side*S(4)}\n              stroke=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.35)\" strokeWidth={2} strokeDasharray=\"6 3\"/>\n            {/* Nacelle EDF pod */}\n            <ellipse cx={x(155)} cy={sy} rx={N_RX} ry={N_RY}\n              fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.12)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={1.5}/>\n            {/* Fan inlet circle */}\n            <circle cx={x(155)} cy={sy} r={S(20)}\n              fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.08)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\"/>\n            {/* Tilt axis indicator */}\n            <line x1={x(130)} y1={sy} x2={x(180)} y2={sy}\n fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>{side<0?\"NACELLE L\":\"NACELLE R\"}</text>\n          </g>\n        );\n      })}\n\n      {/* \u2500\u2500 Engine bell \u2500\u2500 */}\n      <ellipse cx={X_ENGINE_CTR} {/* \u2500\u2500 Antenna markers \u2500\u2500 */}\n      {/* GPS patch */}\n      <rect x={x(46)} y={CY-S(14)} width={S(24)} height={S(10)}\n        fill=\"rgba(74,222,128,0.2)\" stroke=\"#4ade80\" strokeWidth={1}/>\n      <text x={x(58)} y={CY-S(18)} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill=\"#4ade80\" fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>GPS</text>\n      {/* 49MHz dorsal */}\n      <circle cx={x(290)} cy={CY-S(16)}       stroke={C.green} strokeWidth={1} strokeDasharray=\"5 3\"/>\n      <polygon points={`${X_CG},${CY-S(56)} ${X_CG-7},${CY-S(36)} ${X_CG+7},${CY-S(36)}`}\n        fill={C.green} opacity={0.9}/>\n      <text x={X_CG} y={CY-S(62)} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.green} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>CG\u00b7152</text>\n\n      {/* Zone labels */}\n      {sel && zones.filter(z=>z.id===sel).map(z=>(\n        <text key={z.id} x={(z.x1+z.x2)/2} y={CY-S(52)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n          fill={z.c} fontSize={9} fontFamily={M} fontWeight=\"bold\">{z.lbl}</text>\n      ))}\n\n      {/* Dim line */}\n      <line x1={NX} y1={VH-18} x2={X_TAIL} y2={VH-18} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <line x1={NX} y1={VH-22} x2={NX} y2={VH-14} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <line x1={X_TAIL} y1={VH-22} x2={X_TAIL} y2={VH-14} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.25}/>\n      <text x={(NX+X_TAIL)/2} y={VH-7} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>360 mm</text>\n\n      {/* Wingspan dim */}\n      <line x1={NX+S(25)} y1={CY-S(350)} x2={NX+S(25)} y2={CY+S(350)}\n        stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={0.4} opacity={0.15}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(25)-8} y={CY} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}\n        transform={`rotate(-90 ${NX+S(25)-8} ${CY})`}>680mm wingspan</text>\n\n      <text x={VW/2} y={16} textAnchor=\"middle\" fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.25)\"\n        fontSize={9} fontFamily={M} letterSpacing=\"0.12em\">TOP / PLAN VIEW \u2014 CLICK ZONE TO IDENTIFY</text>\n      <text x={NX-8} y={CY+4} textAnchor=\"end\" fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>NOSE</text>\n      <text x={X_TAIL+5} y={CY+4} fill={C.dimmer} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>TAIL</text>\n    </svg>\n  );\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500 SIDE VIEW SVG \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\nfunction SideView(){\n  const VW=680, VH=320, BY=180; // BY = bottom of fuselage baseline\n\n  // Side profile half-heights (above and below centre) at key x stations (mm)\n  // Serenity side: forward cockpit bubble tall, hull sweeps, neck thin, engine bell re-expands\n  const above=[ // top edge\n    [0,0],[5,8],[18,22],[40,32],[58,38],[75,36],\n    [88,30],[110,26],[140,26],[165,25],[195,24],\n    [220,20],[255,12],[270,16],[300,20],[340,18],[360,14],\n  ];\n  const below=[ // bottom edge (belly)\n    [0,0],[10,-5],[35,-14],[88,-20],[140,-22],[180,-22],\n    [220,-20],[255,-14],[270,-18],[300,-22],[340,-20],[360,-14],\n  ];\n  const buildPath=(pts,flip=false)=>{\n    return pts.map(([xmm,ymm],i)=>{\n      const px=NX+S(xmm), py=BY-S(ymm)*(flip?-1:1);\n      return i===0?`M${px},${py}`:`L${px},${py}`;\n    }).join(\" \");\n  };\n  const topEdge=buildPath(above);\n  const botEdge=buildPath(below.map(([x,y])=>[x,-y])); // flip for below\n  const outlineTop=above.map(([xmm,ymm])=>[NX+S(xmm), BY-S(ymm)]);\n  const outlineBot=[...below].reverse().map(([xmm,ymm])=>[NX+S(xmm), BY+S(Math.abs(ymm))]);\n  const allSide=[...outlineTop,...outlineBot];\n  const sidePath=allSide.map((p,i)=>i===0?`M${p[0]},${p[1]}`:`L${p[0]},${p[1]}`).join(\" \")+\"Z\";\n\n  return(\n    <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${VW} ${VH}`} width=\"100%\" style={{maxWidth:\"100%\",display:\"block\"}}>\n      {/* Hull */}\n      <path d={sidePath} fill={C.hull} stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.8}/>\n\n      {/* Cockpit bubble \u2014 the iconic raised dome of the Serenity */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(8)},${BY-S(22)} Q${NX+S(45)},${BY-S(65)} ${NX+S(85)},${BY-S(30)}`}\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.1)\" stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.2}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(44)} y={BY-S(48)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill=\"rgba(0,229,255,0.45)\" fontSize={7} fontFamily={M}>COCKPIT</text>\n\n      {/* Outrigger junction visible as bracket on side */}\n      <line x1={NX+S(130)} y1={BY-S(26)} x2={NX+S(130)} y2={BY-S(60)}\n        stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=\"round\"/>\n      <line x1={NX+S(170)} y1={BY-S(26)} x2={NX+S(170)} y2={BY-S(60)}\n        stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={2} strokeLinecap=\"round\"/>\n      {/* Nacelle side profile \u2014 shown in hover (vertical) position */}\n      <rect x={NX+S(138)} y={BY-S(95)} width={S(24)} height={S(48)} rx={4}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.1)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={1.3}/>\n      {/* Fan inlet at bottom of nacelle in hover */}\n      <ellipse cx={NX+S(150)} cy={BY-S(52)} rx={S(10)} ry={S(4)}\n        fill=\"rgba(255,107,53,0.15)\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8}/>\n      {/* Tilt arc */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(130)},${BY-S(62)} A${S(24)},${S(24)} 0 0,1 ${NX+S(154)},${BY-S(38)}`}\n        fill=\"none\" stroke={C.orange} strokeWidth={0.8} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\" opacity={0.7}/>\n      <text x={NX+S(150)} y={BY-S(102)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.orange} fontSize={6} fontFamily={M}>\u00b190\u00b0</text>\n      <text x={NX+S(150)} y={BY-S(110)} textAnchor=\"middle\"\n        fill={C.orange} fontSize={7} fontFamily={M} fontWeight=\"bold\">NACELLE</text>\n\n      {/* Engine bell \u2014 iconic Serenity exhaust ring */}\n      <path d={`M${NX+S(265)},${BY-S(13)} Q${NX+S(275)},${BY-S(24)} ${NX+S(285)},${BY-S(22)}\n                L${NX+S(330)},${BY-S(22)} Q${NX+S(345)},${BY-S(20)} ${NX+S(355)},${BY-S(15)}\n                L${NX+S(360)},${BY-S(14)} L${NX+S(360)},${BY+S(14)}\n                L${NX+S(355)},${BY+S(15)} Q${NX+S(345)},${BY+S(20)} ${NX+S(330)},${BY+S(22)}\n                L${NX+S(285)},${BY+S(22)} Q${NX+S(275)},${BY+S(24)} <rect x={NX+S(130)} y={BY+S(20)} width={S(70)} height={S(22)} rx={3}\n        fill=\"rgba(244,114,182,0.1)\" stroke={C.pink} strokeWidth={1} strokeDasharray=\"3 2\"/>\n      <text x={NX+S(165)} {[x(95),x(230)].map((sx,i)=>(\n        <g key={i}>\n          <line x1={sx} y1={BY+S(20)} x2={sx-S(8)} y2={BY+S(42)}\n            stroke={C.accent} strokeWidth={1.5} opacity={0.5}/>\n          <line     "text": "Click zones in the top-view diagram to inspect each bay. The Serenity turns out to be a remarkably good functional match \u2014 here's why, and what needed adjusting:\n\n**The one perfect coincidence:** The Serenity's two lateral \"atmo\" engines *already tilt* between horizontal cruise and angled-down landing/hover in the show. This maps exactly to our tilting nacelle EDFs. The circular main drive maps to the fixed forward EDF. The show's designers essentially built a tiltrotor.\n\n**Key adaptations:**\n\nThe original Printables model is ~180mm at display scale and prints solid at 137g. Naively doubling it to 360mm and printing solid would yield ~1,100g of hull alone \u2014 clearly impossible. The engine bell fairing in the Serenity tail grows slightly to accommodate the 35mm duct, but it still reads as the iconic circular drive at this hull scale. It also means the transition to cruise can begin at a slightly lower altitude since there's more margin to catch any altitude loss.\n\n**ESC upgrade to 35A:** The 65mm draws 28A at WOT, so 30A ESCs were marginal. At hover the ESCs sit at only ~30% of their 35A rating \u2014 they'll barely warm up.
